The E.C. number 1.13.11.42 has been deleted in 2006. Instead, replaced with E.C. 1.13.11.11 - tryptophan 2,3-dioxygenase. However, E.C. 1.13.11.11 is for the reaction L-tryptophan + O2 = N-formyl-L-kynurenine. For the reaction 5-Hydroxy-L-tryptophan (Cytosol) + O2 (Cytosol) &lt;=&gt; 5-Hydroxy-N-formylkynurenine, E.C. should be 1.13.11.52. Conclusion: Change E.C. to 1.13.11.52 (source: KEGG).
